FROM (
    SELECT [c].[CustomerID], [c].[CompanyName], [c].[EmailAddress], [c].[FirstName], [c].[LastName], [c].[Phone], (
        SELECT COUNT(*)
        FROM [SalesLT].[CustomerAddress] AS [c0]
